GT Equivalence Verification (CRK3)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three distinct basis functions:
1. `A²` (polynomial)
2. `A*exp(-0.0371*t)` (exponential decay times A)
3. `cos(log(A + 1))` (cosine of logarithm)

The third term `cos(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function. It cannot be exactly represented by polynomials, rational functions, exponentials, or simple logarithms. This is the key discriminator.

Let me check which candidates contain a `cos(log(...))` term or something equivalent:

Scanning all candidates... None of the candidates contain `cos(log(...))` or any cosine function except Candidate 33 which has `sin(c8*t + c9)` (but this is sin of t, not cos of log(A)).

Now, can `cos(log(A+1))` be approximated by any of the basis functions present in the candidates? No - by the linear independence principle, `cos(log(A+1))` cannot be exactly represented by:
- Polynomials in A
- Rational functions of A (like `A/(A+c)`)
- Exponentials in t or A
- `log(A+c)` terms
- `|A|` terms (which equal A for A≥0)
- `sqrt(A)` terms
- `Max(0, A)` terms (which equal A for A≥0)
- `A^c` power terms

The function `cos(log(A+1))` is oscillatory in log-space and cannot be matched by any combination of these basis functions for all A ≥ 0.

Let me verify there's no candidate with cos(log(...)):
- Candidate 33 has `sin(c8*t + c9)` - depends on t, not A
- No other candidate has trigonometric or cos/sin functions

Since `cos(log(A+1))` is linearly independent from all basis functions available in every candidate, and its coefficient (0.7049) is non-zero, no candidate can match the GT exactly.

Let me do a final check: could `cos(log(A+1))` be constant? No, it varies with A. At A=0, cos(log(1))=cos(0)=1. At A=e-1≈1.718, cos(log(e))=cos(1)≈0.540. It's clearly non-constant.

Therefore, no candidate matches.
